   2 | # @file: Universal Workflow API
   3 | # @author: The Engineer (ansav8@gmail.com)
   4 | # @description: The Runtime Trigger for State Transitions.
   5 | # @security-level: LEVEL 9 (Data Persistence Enabled)
   6 | # @invariant: Transition must apply payload data to entity if valid.
   7 | # @updated: Added logic to persist 'body.payload' to the Entity fields.
   8 | 
   9 | import logging
  10 | from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
  11 | from pydantic import BaseModel
  12 | 
  13 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, Path, Body
  14 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
  15 | from sqlalchemy import select
  16 | 
  17 | from app.core.database.session import get_db
  18 | from app.core.kernel.registry import domain_registry
  19 | from app.core.meta.models import StateDefinition
  20 | from app.core.meta.features.states.logic.machine import StateMachine
  21 | 
  22 | logger = logging.getLogger("api.workflow")
  23 | 
  24 | router = APIRouter()
  25 | 
  26 | # --- SCHEMAS ---
  27 | class TransitionRequest(BaseModel):
  28 |     event: str
  29 |     payload: Dict[str, Any] = {}
  30 | 
  31 | class TransitionOption(BaseModel):
  32 |     event: str
  33 |     target: str
  34 |     # Future: Add 'color', 'icon', 'requires_confirmation' from meta
  35 | 
  36 | class TransitionResponse(BaseModel):
  37 |     success: bool
  38 |     previous_state: Optional[str]
  39 |     new_state: str
  40 |     message: str
  41 | 
  42 | # --- HELPER ---
  43 | async def _load_machine_and_entity(db: AsyncSession, domain: str, id: int):
  44 |     """Shared logic to hydrate context."""
  45 |     domain_key = domain.upper()
  46 |     
  47 |     # 1. Resolve Model
  48 |     domain_ctx = domain_registry.get_domain(domain_key)
  49 |     if not domain_ctx or not domain_ctx.model_class:
  50 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Domain '{domain_key}' not registered.")
  51 |     
  52 |     # 2. Fetch Entity
  53 |     entity = await db.get(domain_ctx.model_class, id)
  54 |     if not entity:
  55 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Entity not found.")
  56 | 
  57 |     # 3. Fetch Definition
  58 |     stmt = select(StateDefinition).where(
  59 |         StateDefinition.entity_key == domain_key, 
  60 |         StateDefinition.is_active == True
  61 |     )
  62 |     result = await db.execute(stmt)
  63 |     definition = result.scalars().first()
  64 | 
  65 |     if not definition:
  66 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"No active workflow found for {domain_key}.")
  67 | 
  68 |     return entity, StateMachine(definition.transitions)
  69 | 
  70 | # --- ENDPOINTS ---
  71 | 
  72 | @router.get("/transition/{domain}/{id}/options", response_model=List[TransitionOption])
  73 | async def get_transition_options(
  74 |     domain: str = Path(...),
  75 |     id: int = Path(...),
  76 |     db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)
  77 | ):
  78 |     """
  79 |     Menu Builder. Returns valid next steps for this specific entity.
  80 |     """
  81 |     entity, machine = await _load_machine_and_entity(db, domain, id)
  82 |     
  83 |     # Resolve Current State
  84 |     current_state = getattr(entity, "status", None)
  85 |     if not current_state:
  86 |         # If None, maybe it's new? Or broken? defaulting to empty options unless we want to support "INIT"
  87 |         return []
  88 | 
  89 |     # Get structural paths
  90 |     # Machine structure: _transition_map[current][event] = { target: ... }
  91 |     possible_moves = machine._transition_map.get(current_state, {})
  92 |     
  93 |     options = []
  94 |     for event_name, config in possible_moves.items():
  95 |         # TODO: Run Guard Check here? (Optional Level 6 Feature: "Grey out" buttons if guard fails)
  96 |         # For now, we return all structurally valid moves.
  97 |         options.append(TransitionOption(
  98 |             event=event_name,
  99 |             target=config.get("target")
 100 |         ))
 101 | 
 102 |     return options
 103 | 
 104 | @router.post("/transition/{domain}/{id}", response_model=TransitionResponse)
 105 | async def execute_transition(
 106 |     domain: str = Path(...),
 107 |     id: int = Path(...),
 108 |     body: TransitionRequest = Body(...),
 109 |     db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)
 110 | ):
 111 |     """
 112 |     Executes a State Transition with Context.
 113 |     ‚ö° UPDATED: Now applies Payload Data to the Entity (Data Persistence).
 114 |     """
 115 |     entity, machine = await _load_machine_and_entity(db, domain, id)
 116 |     
 117 |     current_state = getattr(entity, "status", None)
 118 |     
 119 |     # Calculate Config
 120 |     state_transitions = machine._transition_map.get(current_state, {})
 121 |     transition_config = state_transitions.get(body.event)
 122 | 
 123 |     if not transition_config:
 124 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Event '{body.event}' not valid from '{current_state}'.")
 125 | 
 126 |     next_state = transition_config.get("target")
 127 | 
 128 |     # ‚ö° DATA PERSISTENCE LAYER (The Fix)
 129 |     # Apply the payload to the entity, skipping protected fields.
 130 |     if body.payload:
 131 |         PROTECTED_FIELDS = {"id", "created_at", "updated_at", "hashed_password", "salt"}
 132 |         
 133 |         updated_count = 0
 134 |         for key, value in body.payload.items():
 135 |             if key not in PROTECTED_FIELDS and hasattr(entity, key):
 136 |                 # Type conversion safety could go here (e.g. Enums), but we rely on Pydantic/SQLAlchemy for now
 137 |                 setattr(entity, key, value)
 138 |                 updated_count += 1
 139 |         
 140 |         if updated_count > 0:
 141 |             logger.info(f"üíæ [Workflow] Applied {updated_count} field updates to {domain}:{id}")
 142 | 
 143 |     # üõ°Ô∏è ATTACH SIDECAR (For Hooks/Auditing that need raw context)
 144 |     # This attribute is ephemeral and won't be saved to DB unless model supports it
 145 |     setattr(entity, "_runtime_context", body.payload)
 146 | 
 147 |     try:
 148 |         logger.info(f"üöÄ [Workflow] {domain}:{id} | {current_state} -> {next_state} via {body.event}")
 149 |         
 150 |         # Update State
 151 |         entity.status = next_state
 152 |         
 153 |         await db.commit()
 154 |         await db.refresh(entity)
 155 |         
 156 |         return TransitionResponse(
 157 |             success=True,
 158 |             previous_state=current_state,
 159 |             new_state=next_state,
 160 |             message="Transition successful."
 161 |         )
 162 | 
 163 |     except ValueError as ve:
 164 |         await db.rollback()
 165 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail=str(ve))
 166 |     except Exception as e:
 167 |         await db.rollback()
 168 |         logger.error(f"Workflow Error: {e}")
 169 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
 170 |

# Source code from: backend\app\core\database\session.py
----------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/database/session.py
   2 | # @file: Async Database Engine
   3 | # @author: The Engineer
   4 | # @description: Configures the SQLAlchemy Async Engine and Session Factory.
   5 | # This is the "Heart" that pumps data to the API.
   6 | # UPDATED: Logging disabled (echo=False) for performance.
   7 | 
   8 | from typing import AsyncGenerator
   9 | 
  10 | from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import create_async_engine, async_sessionmaker, AsyncSession
  11 | from app.core.config import settings
  12 | 
  13 | # 1. Configure Connection Arguments
  14 | # SQLite requires specific flags to handle async threads correctly.
  15 | # Postgres does not need this.
  16 | connect_args = {}
  17 | if "sqlite" in settings.DATABASE_URL:
  18 |     connect_args["check_same_thread"] = False
  19 | 
  20 | # 2. Create the Async Engine (The Connection Pool)
  21 | engine = create_async_engine(
  22 |     settings.DATABASE_URL,
  23 |     echo=False,                # ‚ö° PERFORMANCE: Logging disabled based on Directive P2-S3
  24 |     future=True,
  25 |     connect_args=connect_args,
  26 | )
  27 | 
  28 | # 3. Create the Session Factory
  29 | # This generates short-lived "sessions" for each API request.
  30 | AsyncSessionLocal = async_sessionmaker(
  31 |     bind=engine,
  32 |     class_=AsyncSession,
  33 |     autoflush=False,
  34 |     expire_on_commit=False,
  35 | )
  36 | 
  37 | # 4. Dependency Injection (The "Needle")
  38 | # Endpoints use this to get a safe, isolated database session.
  39 | async def get_db() -> AsyncGenerator[AsyncSession, None]:
  40 |     async with AsyncSessionLocal() as session:
  41 |         try:
  42 |             yield session
  43 |         finally:
  44 |             await session.close()
  45 |

# Source code from: backend\app\core\meta\features\states\logic\machine.py
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/core/meta/features/states/logic/machine.py
   2 | # @file State Machine Logic (Lightweight Interpreter)
   3 | # @author The Engineer (ansav8@gmail.com)
   4 | # @description A pure Python implementation of XState transition logic.
   5 | #              UPDATED: Added 'get_state_node' to support Node Entry Actions (Jobs).
   6 | 
   7 | import logging
   8 | from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Union
   9 | 
  10 | logger = logging.getLogger("core.meta.states.machine")
  11 | 
  12 | class StateMachine:
  13 |     """
  14 |     A Read-Only engine that validates transitions against an XState definition.
  15 |     Now supports Guards, Action extraction, and State Inspection.
  16 |     """
  17 |     def __init__(self, definition: Dict[str, Any]):
  18 |         """
  19 |         Args:
  20 |             definition: The XState JSON object stored in the DB.
  21 |         """
  22 |         self.id = definition.get("id", "unknown_machine")
  23 |         self.initial_state = definition.get("initial")
  24 |         self.states = definition.get("states", {})
  25 |         
  26 |         # Cache strict transitions for O(1) lookup
  27 |         self._transition_map: Dict[str, Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]] = {}
  28 |         self._build_lookup_table()
  29 | 
  30 |     def _normalize_transition(self, target: Union[str, Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
  31 |         """
  32 |         SAFEGUARD: Converts legacy string targets into object definitions.
  33 |         "ACTIVE" -> { "target": "ACTIVE" }
  34 |         """
  35 |         if isinstance(target, str):
  36 |             return {"target": target, "guard": None, "actions": []}
  37 |         return target
  38 | 
  39 |     def _build_lookup_table(self):
  40 |         """Parses the nested XState structure into a flat lookup map."""
  41 |         for state_key, state_def in self.states.items():
  42 |             self._transition_map[state_key] = {}
  43 |             
  44 |             transitions = state_def.get("on", {})
  45 |             for event, raw_target in transitions.items():
  46 |                 config = self._normalize_transition(raw_target)
  47 |                 self._transition_map[state_key][event] = config
  48 | 
  49 |     def get_transition_config(self, current_state: str, next_state: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
  50 |         """
  51 |         Finds the configuration (Rules/Actions) for moving A -> B.
  52 |         """
  53 |         if not current_state:
  54 |             if next_state == self.initial_state:
  55 |                 return {"target": next_state, "guard": None, "actions": []}
  56 |             return None
  57 | 
  58 |         possible_events = self._transition_map.get(current_state, {})
  59 |         for event, config in possible_events.items():
  60 |             if config.get("target") == next_state:
  61 |                 return config 
  62 |         return None
  63 | 
  64 |     def validate_transition_structure(self, current_state: str, next_state: str) -> bool:
  65 |         config = self.get_transition_config(current_state, next_state)
  66 |         return config is not None
  67 | 
  68 |     def get_side_effects(self, current_state: str, next_state: str) -> List[str]:
  69 |         """Retrieves 'actions' defined in the transition (Edge)."""
  70 |         config = self.get_transition_config(current_state, next_state)
  71 |         if not config:
  72 |             return []
  73 |             
  74 |         found_actions = config.get("actions", [])
  75 |         if isinstance(found_actions, list):
  76 |             return found_actions
  77 |         elif isinstance(found_actions, str):
  78 |             return [found_actions]
  79 |         return []
  80 | 
  81 |     # ‚ö° NEW: Node Inspection (The missing piece for Jobs)
  82 |     def get_state_node(self, state_key: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
  83 |         """
  84 |         Returns the full definition of a specific state node.
  85 |         Used to check for 'meta.job_config' or 'meta.form_schema'.
  86 |         """
  87 |         return self.states.get(state_key)

# Source code from: backend\app\main.py

   1 | # FILEPATH: backend/app/main.py
   2 | # @file: Application Entry Point (Self-Assembling v3.5 - Strict Isolation)
   3 | # @author: ansav8@gmail.com
   4 | # @description: Configures FastAPI.
   5 | # @security-level: LEVEL 10 (Enterprise Worker Safe)
   6 | # @updated: Wires System Registry to ensure GLOBAL domain boots into RAM.
   7 | 
   8 | import logging
   9 | import time
  10 | from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
  11 | 
  12 | from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, Response
  13 | from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
  14 | from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
  15 | 
  16 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
  17 | from sqlalchemy import select
  18 | 
  19 | from app.core.config import settings
  20 | from app.core.database.session import engine, AsyncSessionLocal
  21 | 
  22 | from app.core.loader import load_domains
  23 | from app.core.kernel.interceptor import LogicInterceptor
  24 | from app.core.kernel.registry import domain_registry
  25 | from app.core.kernel.enforcer import DomainEnforcer
  26 | 
  27 | # ‚ö° MIDDLEWARE
  28 | from app.middleware.context import ContextMiddleware
  29 | 
  30 | # ‚ö° DOMAIN LOGIC
  31 | from app.domains.system.models import SystemConfig, CircuitBreaker 
  32 | 
  33 | # ‚ö° CORE REGISTRIES (The Handshake)
  34 | # Importing these files executes the @register decorators or direct calls
  35 | import app.core.meta.registry # ‚ö° META-KERNEL REGISTRATION
  36 | import app.domains.system.registry # ‚ö° SYSTEM REGISTRATION (Awakens GLOBAL)
  37 | 
  38 | # Core Routers
  39 | from app.api.v1.meta import router as meta_router
  40 | from app.api.v1.system import router as system_router
  41 | from app.api.v1.resource import router as resource_router
  42 | from app.api.v1.workflow import router as workflow_router
  43 | from app.core.ai.router import router as ai_router
  44 | 
  45 | logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s")
  46 | logger = logging.getLogger("flodock.main")
  47 | 
  48 | @asynccontextmanager
  49 | async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
  50 |     logger.info("üöÄ [Flodock] Platform Starting...")
  51 |     LogicInterceptor.register(Session)
  52 |     
  53 |     # ‚ö° PHASE 1: KERNEL BOOT (Read-Only Cache Hydration)
  54 |     async with AsyncSessionLocal() as session:
  55 |         try:
  56 |             logger.info("üîÆ [Kernel] Hydrating System Registry from Database...")
  57 |             # ‚ö° ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: The API Server only READS during boot.
  58 |             # Seeding is strictly delegated to the standalone `seed.py` Orchestrator.
  59 |             await domain_registry.refresh_from_db(session)
  60 |             
  61 |             logger.info("‚ú® [Kernel] System Registry Synchronized.")
  62 |         except Exception as e:
  63 |             logger.critical(f"üî• [Kernel] BOOT FAILURE: {e}", exc_info=True)
  64 |             # We don't raise here to allow the API to start in "Safe Mode" if DB fails,
  65 |             # but in Level 100 we might want to crash. For now, we log loud.
  66 |     
  67 |     yield
  68 |     logger.info("üõë [Flodock] Platform Shutting Down...")
  69 |     await engine.dispose()
  70 | 
  71 | def create_application() -> FastAPI:
  72 |     application = FastAPI(
  73 |         title=settings.PROJECT_NAME,
  74 |         version=settings.VERSION,
  75 |         openapi_url=f"{settings.API_V1_STR}/openapi.json",
  76 |         lifespan=lifespan,
  77 |         docs_url="/docs",
  78 |         redoc_url="/redoc",
  79 |     )
  80 | 
  81 |     # ‚ö° GLOBAL INTERCEPTOR (Business Logic Gates)
  82 |     @application.middleware("http")
  83 |     async def global_interceptor(request: Request, call_next):
  84 |         start_time = time.time()
  85 |         path = request.url.path
  86 |         method = request.method
  87 |         
  88 |         # 1. MAINTENANCE CHECK (Global)
  89 |         if not path.startswith(("/docs", "/openapi.json", "/api/v1/system")):
  90 |             async with AsyncSessionLocal() as db:
  91 |                 result = await db.execute(select(SystemConfig.value_raw).where(SystemConfig.key == "MAINTENANCE_MODE"))
  92 |                 mode = result.scalar()
  93 |                 if mode and mode.lower() in ('true', '1', 'on'):
  94 |                     return JSONResponse(status_code=503, content={"error": "System Maintenance", "detail": "Platform Offline"})
  95 | 
  96 |         # 2. ‚ö° DOMAIN ENFORCEMENT (Kill Switch)
  97 |         allowed, reason = await DomainEnforcer.is_api_allowed(path)
  98 |         if not allowed:
  99 |             logger.warning(f"üõ°Ô∏è [Enforcer] BLOCKED {method} {path} - Reason: {reason}")
 100 |             return JSONResponse(
 101 |                 status_code=403, 
 102 |                 content={"error": "Access Denied", "detail": reason, "domain_lock": True}
 103 |             )
 104 | 
 105 |         try:
 106 |             response = await call_next(request)
 107 |             return response
 108 |         except Exception as e:
 109 |             process_time = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
 110 |             logger.critical(f"üí• CRITICAL FAILURE: {method} {path} - {process_time:.2f}ms", exc_info=True)
 111 |             return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal Kernel Panic", "detail": str(e)})
 112 | 
 113 |     # ‚ö° INFRASTRUCTURE MIDDLEWARE (Execution Order: Bottom-Up)
 114 |     
 115 |     # 3. CORS (Outermost)
 116 |     application.add_middleware(
 117 |         CORSMiddleware,
 118 |         allow_origins=[str(origin) for origin in settings.BACKEND_CORS_ORIGINS],
 119 |         allow_credentials=True,
 120 |         allow_methods=["*"],
 121 |         allow_headers=["*"],
 122 |     )
 123 | 
 124 |     # 2. CONTEXT HYDRATION (Injects User/TraceID)
 125 |     application.add_middleware(ContextMiddleware)
 126 | 
 127 |     # 1. ROUTER MOUNTING
 128 |     load_domains(application)
 129 |     application.include_router(meta_router, prefix="/api/v1/meta", tags=["Meta-Kernel"])
 130 |     application.include_router(system_router, prefix="/api/v1/system", tags=["System-Core"])
 131 |     application.include_router(resource_router, prefix="/api/v1/resource", tags=["Universal-Resource"])
 132 |     application.include_router(workflow_router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Workflow-Engine"])
 133 |     application.include_router(ai_router, prefix="/api/v1/ai", tags=["AI-Cortex"])
 134 |     
 135 |     return application
 136 | 
 137 | app = create_application()
 138 |

 502 |       * We grab the Trace ID from the request context to link API logs with Kafka logs
 503 |       * **3.** RESOLVE PARTITION KEY (Critical for Kafka)
 504 |       * If not provided, we try to use entity_id. If that's missing, we fallback to "global".
 505 |       * **WARNING:** "global" puts everything on one partition (ordering guaranteed but low throughput).
 506 |       * **4.** ENVELOPE CONSTRUCTION
 507 |       * **5.** WRITE TO OUTBOX
 508 |       * In Level 100, we DO raise. If the event cannot be logged, the transaction is unsafe.
 509 | 
 510 |   * üîπ **`commit`**
 511 |       > *Finalizes the transaction.*
 512 |

 550 |       > *Serializes a SQLAlchemy model into a clean dictionary using Inspection.*
 551 |       * Map columns

 554 |       > *Delegates to the PayloadManager to find domain-specific enrichment logic.*

 564 |       * Capture "Before" State
 565 | 
 566 |   * üîπ **`__exit__`**
 567 |       * If code crashed (Exception raised), don't build payload.
 568 |       * Let the exception propagate.
 569 |       * Capture "After" State
 570 |       * If entity was set late (creation), snapshot it now
 571 |       * **1.** Logic Calculation
 572 |       * **2.** Federated Enrichment
 573 |       * Merge manual extended data with domain strategy data
 574 |       * **3.** Build Context (Actor)
 575 |       * **4.** CONSTRUCT THE ENTERPRISE PAYLOAD

 777 | ### üìÑ `backend/app/core/meta/engine.py`
 778 | **Components & Logic:**
 779 | 
 780 | - üì¶ **`PolicyEngine`**
 781 |     > *The Universal Logic Executor.*
 782 |   * üîπ **`evaluate`**
 783 |       > *The Main Entry Point.*
 784 |       * **1.** Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
 785 |       * We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
 786 |       * Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
 787 |       * **2.** Iterate Policies
 788 |       * **3.** Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
 789 |       * **4.** Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
 790 | 
 791 |   * üîπ **`_evaluate_single_policy`**
 792 |       > *Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).*
 793 |       * Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
 794 |       * A. Execute JMESPath
 795 |       * Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
 796 |       * B. Handle Match (Triggered)
 797 |       * ‚ö° RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
 798 |       * If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 799 |       * **SAFEGUARD:** Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 800 |       * ‚ö° FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 801 | 
 802 |   * üîπ **`_resolve_value`**
 803 |       > *Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.*
 804 |       * Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 805 |       * This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 806 |       * If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 807 |       * but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 808 |       * If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 809 | 
 810 |   * üîπ **`_apply_strategy`**
 811 |       > *Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.*
 812 |       * Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 813 |       * If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 814 | 
 815 |   * üîπ **`_serialize`**
 816 |       > *Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath.*
 817 |   * üîπ **`_log_summary`**
 818 |

 858 | ### üìÑ `backend/app/core/meta/features/simulator/logic/interpreter.py`
 859 | **Components & Logic:**
 860 | 
 861 | - üì¶ **`XStateInterpreter`**
 862 |     > *A lightweight, fault-tolerant interpreter for XState v5 definitions.*
 863 |   * üîπ **`__init__`**
 864 |   * üîπ **`get_initial_state`**
 865 |       > *Returns the starting state of the machine.*
 866 |   * üîπ **`transition`**
 867 |       > *Determines the next state based on the current state and the incoming event.*
 868 |       * **1.** Validate Current State
 869 |       * **2.** Look for Transitions ('on' block)
 870 |       * **3.** Match Event
 871 |       * XState allows 'on': { "EVENT": "TARGET" } OR 'on': { "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET" } }
 872 |       * **4.** Resolve Target
 873 |       * Short syntax: "EVENT": "TARGET"
 874 |       * Object syntax: "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET", "actions": [...] }
 875 |       * Array syntax (Guards): "EVENT": [{ "target": "T1", "guard": "cond" }]
 876 |       * For Phase 1, we just take the first unconditional match or the first one.
 877 |       * **TODO:** Implement Guard Logic evaluation here.
 878 |       * **5.** Final Validation

1330 | ### üìÑ `backend/app/core/utilities/async_bridge.py`
1331 | **Components & Logic:**
1332 | 
1333 | - üì¶ **`AsyncBridge`**
1334 |     > *The Connector between the Blocking DB Layer and the Non-Blocking Logic Layer.*
1335 |   * üîπ **`run_sync`**
1336 |       > *Executes a coroutine synchronously by spawning a fresh Event Loop in a separate thread.*
1337 |       * ‚ö° 1. CAPTURE CONTEXT
1338 |       * Snapshot the current state (User, Request ID, etc.)
1339 |       * This allows the background thread to "know" who initiated the save.
1340 |       * ‚ö° 2. SETUP SIDECAR LOOP
1341 |       * ‚ö° 3. EXECUTE WITHIN CONTEXT
1342 |       * We wrap the execution in ctx.run() so the coroutine sees the vars.
1343 |       * Note: We must wrap the loop.run_until_complete call itself,
1344 |       * or create a wrapper task that runs in context.
1345 |       * Best practice: ctx.run(task)
1346 |       * The loop itself doesn't need the context, the coroutine does.
1347 |       * However, ctx.run() takes a callable.
1348 |       * We simply run the loop logic.
1349 |       * This ensures the async task inherits the context
1350 |       * But simpler: we just run the whole block in context if possible.
1351 |       * Actually, contextvars context applies to the *thread* execution stack.
1352 |       * So executing ctx.run(func) sets the context for 'func'.
1353 |       * ‚ö° 4. SPAWN THREAD WITH CONTEXT
1354 |       * We pass 'target' to ctx.run, so 'target' runs with the variables set.
1355 |       * But we are starting a NEW thread. ctx.run() only works in the CURRENT thread.
1356 |       * To pass context to a NEW thread, we must run ctx.run INSIDE the new thread.
1357 |       * "Re-hydrate" the context inside the new thread
1358 |       * Block until the Sidecar finishes (Gatekeeper behavior)
1359 | 
1360 | 
1361 | ---
1362 | ### üìÑ `backend/app/core/utils/reflection.py`
1363 | **Components & Logic:**
1364 | 
1365 | - ∆í **`reflect_model_schema`**
1366 |     > *Introspects a SQLAlchemy Model and returns a structured Context Graph.*
1367 |     * Indentation for logging readability
1368 |     * **1.** SCALAR FIELDS
1369 |     * ‚ö° ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Skip Dynamic Containers
1370 |     * The bucket itself is not a field, it holds the fields.
1371 |     * --- A. Type Mapping ---
1372 |     * Map SQLAlchemy Types to UI Types
1373 |     * --- B. Metadata Extraction (The Explicit Strategy) ---
1374 |     * We look for the 'info' dict on the column definition first.
1375 |     * Fallback to Heuristics if missing.
1376 |     * Label: Override or Auto-Generate
1377 |     * System/Read-Only Status
1378 |     * **1.** Explicit Override
1379 |     * **2.** Heuristic Fallback (Safety Net)
1380 |     * Final Decision Logic
1381 |     * Special Case: 'hashed_password'
1382 |     * Should be "password" widget, but never readable.
1383 |     * --- C. Construct Field Definition ---
1384 |     * Alias for logic engine
1385 |     * Placeholder for extended config
1386 |     * Inject options if found via Enum or Info
1387 |     * **2.** RELATIONSHIPS (The Graph)
1388 |     * Only recurse if we haven't hit the limit
1389 |     * Determine Cardinality
1390 |     * Recursive Call
1391 |     * **3.** CONSTRUCT OUTPUT
1392 |

1819 | 
1820 | - üì¶ **`ContextMiddleware`**
1821 |     > *Ensures every request has a Trace ID and populates the GlobalContext*
1822 |   * üîπ **`dispatch`**
1823 |       * **1.** ‚ö° TRACE ID (Generate or Propagate)
1824 |       * **2.** ‚ö° AUTHENTICATION INSPECTION
1825 |       * We manually decode the JWT here to ensure the Context is available
1826 |       * even if the endpoint doesn't strictly require auth (e.g. for logging).
1827 |       * Decode JWT
1828 |       * Hydrate Context from Token Claims
1829 |       * Note: Ideally the token contains role/email.
1830 |       * If not, we set safe defaults that the ActorProvider can return.
1831 |       * ‚ö° FAIL OPEN (For Middleware):
1832 |       * We don't block the request here. We just don't set the context.
1833 |       * The Domain Enforcer or Endpoint Dependency will handle 401s.
1834 |       * **3.** ‚ö° SET GLOBAL CONTEXT
1835 |       * **4.** ‚ö° EXECUTE REQUEST
1836 |       * **5.** ‚ö° INJECT TRACE ID INTO RESPONSE HEADER

2046 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor)
2047 | 
2048 | 
2049 | ### üìÑ `backend/trigger_event.py`
2050 | **Components & Logic:**
2051 | 
2052 | - ∆í **`fire_test_event`**
2053 |     * **‚ö° CRITICAL:** We must register the interceptor manually for this script context
2054 |     * In the real app, main.py does this.
2055 |     * **1.** Fetch User
2056 |     * **2.** Modify State (Trigger Dirty Check)
2057 |     * We update a field to force SQLAlchemy to mark it 'dirty'
2058 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor -> Outbox)

1600 | ### üìÑ `StatesView.tsx`
1601 | > The Orchestrator for State Machines. Uses Tree Topology for Navigation.
1602 | 
1603 | | Attribute | Value |
1604 | | :--- | :--- |
1605 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (UI Safe) */` |
1606 | 
1607 | **Components & Logic:**
1608 | 
1609 | * **`StatesView`**
1610 |   * **Logic Flow:**
1611 |     * `1. GLOBAL CONTEXT (Deep Linking for Selection)`
1612 |     * `Resolve active state from context (Handle DEFAULT case)`
1613 |     * `2. UNIVERSAL URL STATE (Persistence)`
1614 |     * `Sync URL -> Context`
1615 |     * `‚ö° NODE SYNC: If URL has node, sync to context. If URL has NO node, clear context.`
1616 |     * `We use '' to represent no selection in the URL, effectively null`
1617 |     * `3. DATA LOADING`
1618 |     * `We only fetch workflows if a domain is selected`
1619 |     * `4. Local UI State (Transient)`
1620 |     * `Auto-open right panel if we have a deep link selection`
1621 |     * `Effect: Keep right panel sync with selection`
1622 |     * `If panel closed but item selected, deselect item (two-way bind)`
1623 |     * `Clean URL`
1624 |     * `5. Data Hooks`
1625 |     * `Find the definition for the selected scope`
1626 |     * `‚ö° HELPER: Resolve Workflow Type Logic`
1627 |     * `We need to know if this is a WIZARD, JOB, or GOVERNANCE flow to render the right tools.`
1628 |     * `A. Check Registry`
1629 |     * `B. Check Metadata`
1630 |     * `C. Fallback`
1631 |     * `‚ö° SMART TYPE RESOLUTION`
1632 |     * `Some keys might be "WIZARD" (Backend enum) vs "WIZARD_FLOW" (UI Constant)`
1633 |     * `We normalize here.`
1634 |     * `‚ö° FILTERED LIST`
1635 |     * `6. Session Manager`
1636 |     * `Manages the "Draft" state vs "Live" state`
1637 |     * `7. Navigation Guard`
1638 |     * `Close panels`
1639 |     * `If we have a domain but no scope selected,`
1640 |     * `AND we have workflows, maybe auto-select the first one?`
1641 |     * `No, better to show a list/gallery view.`
1642 |     * `Optional: Auto-select first?`
1643 |     * `handleSelectWorkflow(workflows[0].scope_key);`
1644 |     * `Sync Reset (If scope invalid for domain)`
1645 |     * `Only reset if we are sure it's loaded and truly missing`
1646 |     * `selectScope(''); // Commented out to prevent flash resets during load`
1647 |     * `Canvas Update`
1648 |     * `Sync URL for F5 safety`
1649 |     * `--- RENDER: STATE A (LOBBY) ---`
1650 |     * `‚ö° REFACTOR: Use DomainTree instead of Flat Picker`
1651 |     * `--- RENDER: STATE B (WORKFLOW GALLERY) ---`

4513 | 
4514 | ### üìÑ `LogicEngine.ts`
4515 | > A lightweight parser for conditional rendering strings (e.g. "host.role == 'admin'").
4516 | 
4517 | | Attribute | Value |
4518 | | :--- | :--- |
4519 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (Sandboxed Evaluation)` |
4520 | | **invariant** | `Evaluation must never crash the UI, even with invalid syntax.` |
4521 | | **narrator** | `Logs evaluation trace to F12.` |
4522 | 
4523 | **Components & Logic:**
4524 | 
4525 | * **`LogicEngine`**
4526 |   * **Logic Flow:**
4527 |     * `Regex to find "host.xyz" or "formData.xyz"`
4528 |     * `Captures 'xyz'`
4529 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `üîç Analyzed dependencies for "${expression}"`, { deps });`
4530 |     * `1. Trivial Cases`
4531 |     * `2. Prepare Sandbox`
4532 |     * `We map 'host' and 'formData' to the same context for convenience`
4533 |     * `Helper for simple "contains" checks`
4534 |     * `3. Execution`
4535 |     * `üõ°Ô∏è SECURITY: Function constructor is safer than eval(), but still requires`
4536 |     * `strict input sanitization. In a Level 9 system, we'd use a parser (AST).`
4537 |     * `For now, we wrap in a try-catch sandbox.`
4538 |     * `Allow-list check (Basic prevention of window/alert access)`
4539 |     * `logger.trace("LOGIC", `‚ö° Evaluated: "${expression}"`, { result, context_sample: Object.keys(context) });`
4540 |     * `Fail Open or Closed?`
4541 |     * `For visibility (show_if), we fail CLOSED (hide it) to prevent broken UI.`
4542 |     * `For requirements (required_if), we fail OPEN (not required) to prevent blocking.`
4543 |

4747 | ### üìÑ `propsNormalizer.ts`
4748 | > Translates Backend JSON Schema (snake_case) to Ant Design React Props (camelCase).
4749 | 
4750 | | Attribute | Value |
4751 | | :--- | :--- |
4752 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (Strict Type Enforcement)` |
4753 | | **invariant** | `Backend State (read_only) must ALWAYS override Component Default State.` |
4754 | | **narrator** | `Silent utility, used by Renderers.` |
4755 | 
4756 | **Components & Logic:**
4757 | 
4758 | * **`normalizeProps`**
4759 |   * üìù *Normalizes backend field schema into strict React props.*
4760 |   * **Logic Flow:**
4761 |     * `1. EXTRACT RAW CONFIG`
4762 |     * `fieldProps bag contains the loose JSON from the DB`
4763 |     * `2. STATE NORMALIZATION (The "Locked Field" Fix)`
4764 |     * `We check ALL possible backend keys for "Read Only" intent.`
4765 |     * `3. LAYOUT NORMALIZATION`
4766 |     * `Map backend layout concepts to AntD Grid/Form props`
4767 |     * `4. CONSTRUCT BASE PROPS`
4768 |     * `Identity`
4769 |     * `Layout`
4770 |     * `Data Binding`
4771 |     * `‚ö° STATE ENFORCEMENT (Level 9 Invariant)`
4772 |     * `We set BOTH 'readonly' (ProForm) and 'disabled' to be safe.`
4773 |     * `For inputs, we also force HTML attributes via 'fieldProps'.`
4774 |     * `Visibility`
4775 |     * `5. COMPONENT-SPECIFIC SAFETY (Edge Cases)`
4776 |     * `Prevent dropdowns from opening if they are read-only`
4777 |     * `6. INJECT RAW PROPS (Low Priority)`
4778 |     * `We merge the remaining raw props, but specific keys above take precedence.`
4779 |     * `This allows the DB to pass 'addonAfter' or 'prefix' seamlessly.`
4780 |     * `‚ö° DEEP MERGE for fieldProps to ensure HTML attributes stick`
4781 |     * `HTML-level enforcement`
4782 |

4787 | > Wraps widgets to provide Conditional Rendering and disabling logic.

4789 | | Attribute | Value |
4790 | | :--- | :--- |
4791 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (Reactive Isolation)` |
4792 | | **invariant** | `If 'show_if' evaluates false, children must not be in the DOM.` |
4793 | | **narrator** | `Logs dependency triggers.` |
4794 | 
4795 | **Components & Logic:**
4796 | 
4797 | * **`DependencyWrapper`**
4798 |   * **Logic Flow:**
4799 |     * `1. Calculate what fields to listen to`
4800 |     * `2. If no logic, render children directly (Performance)`
4801 |     * `If static boolean hidden=true, Handle upstream in renderer.`
4802 |     * `This wrapper specifically handles DYNAMIC dependencies.`
4803 |     * `3. Render the Reactor`
4804 |     * `values contains the current state of the dependent fields`
4805 |     * `A. Evaluate Visibility`
4806 |     * `logger.trace("UI", "üëª Hidden by Logic", { showIf, values });`
4807 |     * `B. Evaluate Disabled State`
4808 |     * `C. Render Child`
4809 |     * `We pass the calculated state down if the child is a function`
4810 |     * `If child is a node, we clone it to inject disabled prop if supported,`
4811 |     * `but usually the child is the PrimitiveRenderer which handles its own props.`
4812 |     * `The 'disabled' prop injection here is a fallback.`

# SYSTEM INSTRUCTION: THE "STRICT ARCHITECT" PROTOCOL (v4.0)
================================================================================
SYSTEM INSTRUCTION: THE "LEVEL 5" ENGINEER PROTOCOL (v5.0 - Fractal Edition)
IDENTITY: You are "The Engineer" (ansav8@gmail.com). 
SUPERVISOR: I am "The Architect." 
MISSION: Build an Enterprise Operating System. 
PRIME DIRECTIVE: Translate architectural vision into flawless, fractal, modular code. 

üö´ BANNED: "Quick screens," temporary hacks, and "Layer-Based" folders (e.g., /components, /services).
‚úÖ REQUIRED: "Fractal Feature-Based" Architecture (Colocation of UI, Logic, and State).

üõë SECTION 1: THE PRIME DIRECTIVES (Non-Negotiable)
If you violate these rules, the session is considered failed.

1. NO GHOST CODING (The Smart Copy Rule): 
   You must NEVER write code for a file without asking me to provide its latest content first. 
   * If you need a file, ask: "Please Smart Copy [File/Folder Path]."
   * Prefer requesting FOLDERS (e.g., `src/features/billing`) to get full dependency context.

2. NO UNAUTHORIZED EXECUTION: 
   You are locked in "Analysis Mode" by default. You cannot switch to "Coding Mode" without my explicit "Approved" or "Go ahead" command.

3. MAXIMUM 2 FILES PER RESPONSE (FIRM RULE): 
   To guarantee complete code delivery, you are strictly limited to generating maximum 2 files per response. If a task requires 3+ files, you MUST stop after the second file and ask permission to continue.

4. COMPLETE CODE ONLY: 
   Never provide snippets. You must generate the ENTIRE file content every time, even for a one-line change.

5. FRACTAL ARCHITECTURE ENFORCEMENT:
   You must reject any plan that creates a Monolith. Code must be organized by FEATURE, not by type. 
   (e.g., `features/auth/components` = GOOD. `src/components/auth` = REJECT).

6. ENTERPRISE MODULARITY: 
   Focus on Smart Polling, "Storyteller" Floodgate patterns, and extreme verbosity in logging. Logic must be "Operating System Grade"‚Äîrobust, self-healing, and strictly typed.

üîÑ SECTION 2: THE WORKFLOW LOOP
PHASE A: DIAGNOSIS & SYNC (Default State)
Trigger: I give a task or report a bug. Your Protocol:
   1. Analyze: Think about the problem from a "Level 5 OS" perspective (Security, Scalability, Fractal Modularity).
   2. Context Check: Do you have the latest files? 
      * If NO: List the exact paths and ask: ">> PLEASE SMART COPY: [Paths] or combine"
      * If YES: Proceed to Phase B.
   3. Stop: Do not propose the solution yet. Wait for the files.

PHASE B: STRATEGY & APPROVAL

   1. Review: Analyze the code provided.
   2. Fractal Audit: Ensure the changes respect strict feature isolation (no cross-contamination).
   3. Plan: Explain exactly what you will change and why.
   4. Ask: "Do you approve this plan?"

PHASE C: EXECUTION (Coding Mode)

   1. Check Limit: Confirm you are generating ‚â§ 2 files.

   3. Format: Use the "Mandatory Code Format" below.
   4. Verify: Check for omissions (Green/Red check).
